### [211] [Scalable Policy Optimization for Networked Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Continuous State-Action Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18554)
*Dongming Wang,Pengcheng Dai,Wenwu Yu,Wei Ren*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出连续分布式耦合策略梯度算法(CDCPG)，用于连续状态-动作空间的网络化马尔可夫决策过程协同强化学习，通过局部化贝尔曼理论、谱随机特征表示和自适应邻域选择，实现了与网络规模无关的计算通信复杂度，并证明了$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-2})$的样本复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布式强化学习方法多局限于离散状态动作空间或全网络通信，缺乏面向连续空间网络化MDP的高效协同算法，且存在截断核不匹配、维度障碍等理论问题。

Method: 提出CDCPG算法：每个智能体维护局部演员（限定在图邻域内）和局部最小二乘时序差分评论家（通过谱随机特征近似局部转移核）；构建基于条件期望的截断动作值函数以解决核不匹配问题；证明归一化随机特征的无条件激励界；设计自适应邻域选择规则。

Result: 在智能体交互指数衰减、激励条件和目标平滑性假设下，CDCPG以$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-2})$共享样本驱动每个智能体平均驻留度达到$\varepsilon$精度（匹配非凸光滑一阶率），计算通信复杂度由邻域大小而非网络规模决定；在线性二次型基准实验中验证了局部性和特征维度预测。

Conclusion: CDCPG为连续空间网络化MDP提供了首个理论完备的局部化协同强化学习算法，通过条件期望截断解决了核匹配问题，并建立了可监控的激励条件，实现了网络规模无关的可扩展性。

Abstract: We develop the Continuous Distributed Coupled Policy Gradient (CDCPG) algorithm for cooperative reinforcement learning in networked Markov decision processes with continuous state and action spaces. Each agent maintains a local actor over a bounded graph neighborhood, and a localized least-squares temporal-difference critic evaluates a truncated action-value function through a spectral random-feature representation of the local transition kernel. The analysis makes four contributions. First, the truncated action-value function is constructed as a conditional expectation over the neighborhood, yielding a well-posed localized Bellman theory that removes the continuation-kernel mismatch of naive truncation arguments. Second, we expose a dimensional obstruction to temporal-difference stability for normalized random features and prove an unconditional excitation bound that reduces stability to a symmetric persistence-of-excitation condition, monitorable through an online matrix-concentration certificate. Third, under exponential spatial decay of agent interactions, the excitation condition, and smoothness of the objective, CDCPG drives an averaged per-agent stationarity measure to within any excess $ε$ of an explicitly characterized approximation floor using $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ shared-oracle samples, and the excess dependence matches the smooth nonconvex first-order rate; per-agent computation and communication are governed by the neighborhood size rather than the network size. Fourth, an adaptive-locality rule selects the radius that balances truncation and graph-decay residuals against the target accuracy. Experiments on a networked linear-quadratic benchmark corroborate the locality and feature-dimension predictions.

</details>


### [212] [Strategy-Following Multi-Agent Deep Reinforcement Learning Considering Control Strategies Provided to Other Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18719)
*Yamato Takahagi,Gentoku Nakasone,Yoshinari Motokawa,Toshiharu Sugawara*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出一种多智能体学习新方法，允许人类管理员在训练后通过指令控制部分智能体，未受指令的智能体则能根据环境自适应地补充完成剩余任务，实现更灵活高效的多智能体协作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习多智能体系统在实际应用中，人类难以简单控制训练好的智能体来应对环境和社会变化；同时，向所有智能体下发指令的方式耗时且难以设计最优协作方案，需要更灵活的指令机制。

Method: 扩展了先前在多智能体深度强化学习中可控性的研究工作，提出一种学习框架，使得部分智能体接收关键指令，其余未受指令的智能体能够自适应地补充被忽略的任务和区域。

Result: 实验结果显示，使用所提方法的智能体能够转换到另一种协作结构，并且在性能上优于传统方法。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了更自然的人机协作：人类只需对关键智能体下达指令，其余智能体可自动补位，从而提升多智能体系统的实用性和灵活性。

Abstract: This study proposes a learning method for multi-agent systems that allows agents to be controlled through human manager instructions after learning and enables uninstructed agents to implicitly complement the overall work based on the actions of other agents. Multi-agent applications using deep learning have shown potential; thus, to achieve extensive social applications, humans should be able to control learned agents using simple methods to respond to environmental and social changes. Even without such changes, learned coordination often does not match the expectations of human managers, making it preferable to control coordination structures to match human intentions. Some studies have aimed to control agent behavior using simple instructions. However, they assumed that instructions are provided to all agents, which is time-consuming and not evident when designing a better cooperation regime. Ideally, specific agents should receive key action instructions, while others should automatically complete the remaining tasks. The proposed method, which extends previous work on controllability in multi-agent deep reinforcement learning, enables uninstructed agents to adaptively complement overlooked tasks and areas. The experimental results show that agents using the proposed method can shift to another cooperative structure and achieve better performance than those using conventional methods.

</details>

### [213] [Binding Drift in Multi-Step Tool-Augmented Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18316)
*Rahul Suresh Babu,Shashank Indukuri*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究工具增强语言模型在多步工作流中的实体绑定问题，发现实体锁定会放大错误（3倍），而基于LLM的重新验证器可减少79%的错误，接近理论最优水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作发现单步操作中代理选择正确工具但绑定错误实体的情况占24-26%，但多步场景下实体绑定会如何演变（保持正确、无声漂移、错误传播）尚不清楚。

Method: 形式化区分了绑定漂移（初始正确后变错）和错误传播（初始错误向前传递），在200个工作流、580个实体绑定评分步骤、8种模型上进行了控制实验，包括错误注入和自然场景测试。

Result: (1) 实体锁定策略将错误从907放大到2746（3倍）；(2) Claude Opus 4.5上放大达8.5倍；(3) LLM重新验证器减少79%错误，接近理论最优；(4) 自然场景中基线代理在18%的工作流上发生漂移。

Conclusion: 持久化绑定和重新验证不可互换：消除漂移的防御可能加剧错误传播，而实用的重新验证器几乎能匹配理论最优恢复效果。

Abstract: Tool-augmented language-model agents execute multi-step workflows over external systems, resolving an entity once and then acting on it across subsequent steps. Prior work shows that in single-step actions, agents select the correct tool but bind it to the wrong entity 24-26% of the time. We study what happens to entity bindings over time: do they stay correct, silently drift to a different entity, or, if wrong from the start, propagate and compound? We formalize binding drift (correct at step 1, wrong later) as distinct from error propagation (wrong at step 1, carried forward), and score them on disjoint workflow sets so the two cannot be conflated. In a controlled multi-step testbed (200 workflows, 580 entity-binding-scored steps, four enterprise domains, eight model backends spanning small to frontier), we find: (1) under controlled error injection, an entity lock (the intuitive "persist the first binding" fix) amplifies wrong actions from 907 to 2,746 (3.0x; bootstrap 95% CI [2.8, 3.3]), because it faithfully carries the seeded wrong entity into every later step; (2) the amplification reaches 8.5x on the most affected model (Claude Opus 4.5); (3) a practical LLM-based re-verifier (a single cheap second model call re-reading the original instruction) reduces wrong actions by 79% (0.21x; CI [0.18, 0.25]), closing the gap to within 1 percentage point of an oracle upper-bound (0.20x); and (4) in the natural (non-injected) setting, baseline agents drift on 18% of eligible workflows, with the per-step error rate rising across steps. Persistence and re-verification are not interchangeable: a defense that eliminates drift can worsen propagation, and a practical re-verifier nearly matches oracle recovery.

</details>

*Dimitrios S. Sfiris*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种协议无关的电子商务代理架构，通过规范信封、七轴生成声明门和十一项语义不变量，确保代理在授权支付下的安全交易；在66/66测试中通过评估，验证了依赖变更检测和过期决策预防等核心机制的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计科学研究方法，构建了规范信封、受保护的依赖与结果哈希、Ed25519或HMAC认证、实时请求重新绑定、七轴生成声明门、执行时依赖重新验证以及十一项语义不变量。通过开源JavaScript实现、八个确定性电商场景和五个受控消融实验进行评估。

Conclusion: 研究支持受保护依赖变更检测、有界结果推导、过期决策预防、表面绑定状态一致性、拒绝传播和验证状态身份，但未证明规则完备性、生产安全性、性能、法律合规性、实时互操作性、总体错误率或独立复现。

Abstract: Agentic commerce extends agentic shopping into software agents that interpret policy, prepare checkout, generate transaction-facing language, and act under delegated payment authority. Protocols standardize external exchanges, but merchants still need one authoritative representation of commercial eligibility, actor authority, checkout validity, payment dispatch, generated claims, and evidence. This design-science study presents a protocol-agnostic architecture built around a canonical envelope, protected dependency and result hashes, Ed25519 or HMAC authentication, live-request rebinding, a seven-axis generated-claim gate, execution-time dependency revalidation, and eleven semantic invariants. Evaluation used an open-source JavaScript implementation, eight deterministic ecommerce scenarios, and five controlled ablations. Seven initially valid actions were permitted. After protected state changed, none could proceed without a fresh decision; a hostile-accessor case also remained blocked. Action status was consistent across configured surface-bound envelopes, and each scenario contained the three protected hashes and its targeted dependency reference. Each ablation produced the predicted unsafe regression when one safeguard was bypassed, while the protected path contained the same failure. The hostile accessor was read once, and the suite passed 66/66 tests, schema validation, and committed examples. Results support protected-dependency change detection, bounded outcome derivation, stale-decision prevention, surface-bound status consistency, refusal propagation, and verified-state identity under synthetic fixtures, but do not establish rule completeness, production security, performance, legal compliance, live interoperability, population error rates, or independent replication.

### [215] [CODENS: Transforming Code Changes into Living, Accessible, and Queryable Documentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18356)
*Abdelhak Kelious,Chyrine Tahri,Eliot Bardet*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CODENS是一个将拉取请求自动转化为可查询、可演进的代码知识图谱的系统，支持仓库级别的问答和文档维护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在快速迭代的代码仓库中，设计知识分散在源文件和拉取请求中，导致文档难以保持最新。

Result: 在客户Ruby on Rails生产项目上评估，CODENS生成高度相关且有理有据的答案，但定性反馈指出在简洁、面向文档的合成方面仍存在挑战。

Abstract: Maintaining up-to-date code documentation is difficult in fast-moving repositories because design knowledge is scattered across source files and pull requests. We present CODENS , a system that turns pull requests into living, accessible, and queryable documentation for production codebases. CODENS incrementally builds a typed software knowledge graph from pull requests, enriches components through schema-driven semantic extraction, derives typed relations between them, and exposes the resulting knowledge through three retrieval modes, including agent-guided graph traversal for repository-level question answering. The system also preserves semantic change history across pull requests and integrates both answer-quality and operational evaluation metrics. We evaluate CODENS on a client Ruby on Rails project in production. Results show that CODENS produces highly relevant and well-grounded answers, while qualitative feedback highlights a remaining challenge in concise, documentation-oriented synthesis.

### [216] [Beyond Resolved Rate: A Non-Functional Quality Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18462)
*Xin Sun,Daniel Ståhl,Kristian Sandahl,Christoph Kessler*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在仓库级代码修复任务中，后期模型相较于早期模型是否在生成功能正确补丁的同时，具备更好的非功能质量特性。通过对Claude和DeepSeek模型在SWE-bench Lite上的实验分析发现，后期模型虽然在解决实例数量上有所提升，但在静态分析、CPU时间、内存使用等非功能指标上并未表现出显著或一致的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仓库级编码基准主要关注模型功能正确性（解决率）的进步，忽视了补丁的非功能质量（如代码可维护性、性能等）是否随模型代际更迭而改善。本文旨在填补这一空白，推动对模型实际软件工程能力的更全面评估。

Method: 选取Claude和DeepSeek两个模型家族共四个模型，在SWE-bench Lite上进行两案例研究。使用相同的SWE-agent功能性修复设置，通过CodeQL、CodeScene、CPU时间和峰值内存来评估生成的补丁。主要分析聚焦于模型共同解决的实例，并进行统计显著性检验和多重比较校正（Holm校正）。

Result: 静态分析中，多数CodeQL对差异为零，且所有CodeQL和CodeScene比较经Holm校正后均不显著。CPU时间差异较小且在不同模型家族间不一致，后期模型在基准测试负载下峰值内存略高但绝对差异很小。个别CodeQL规则和CodeScene类别的差异在各模型家族间不一致，且未通过多重比较校正。

Conclusion: 后期模型虽然解决了更多实例，但在共同解决的任务上，测量的非功能指标并未显示出一致性的改进。研究呼吁对模型进行更全面的实际软件工程能力评估。

Abstract: Repository-level coding benchmarks typically measure progress in model capability by comparing the resolved rates of later and earlier models. However, this focus overlooks whether the non-functional quality of their generated patches has also changed across model generations. This study investigates whether later models produce functionally correct patches with better non-functional characteristics than earlier models on comparable repository-level repair tasks. We conducted two case studies involving four Claude and DeepSeek models on SWE-bench Lite. Using the same SWE-agent functional repair setting, we evaluated the generated patches with CodeQL, CodeScene, CPU time, and peak memory. Our primary analysis compared the models on commonly resolved instances. The static analysis results showed that most CodeQL paired differences were zero and that no CodeQL or CodeScene comparison remained significant after Holm correction. CPU time differences were small and inconsistent across model families, while peak memory usage was slightly higher for the later models under the benchmark test workload, with small absolute differences. Differences in individual CodeQL rules and CodeScene categories varied across model families and did not survive multiple-comparison correction. Overall, later models resolved more instances but showed no consistent improvement in the measured non-functional indicators on tasks solved by both models. Through this study, we hope to encourage a more comprehensive evaluation of models' practical software engineering capabilities.

### [217] [Semantic Drift in Bug Resolution: How Behavioral Signals Propagate from Reports to Tests and Patches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18550)
*Wendkûuni C. Ouédraogo,Yinghua Li,Xueqi Dang,Paweł Borsukiewicz,Liang Xiao,Lingfeng Bao,Anil Koyuncu,Jacques Klein,David Lo,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Desc2Fix框架，通过结构化行为锚点和多种相似度指标，量化缺陷报告、触发测试和补丁之间的语义对齐程度。基于2857个三元组和LLM分析发现：对齐可测量但不能简化为相似度，LLM存在系统性乐观偏差，结构化锚点结合嵌入代理能提供可复现的信号用于测试排序和补丁筛选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷修复是跨工件的流程，但自然语言报告中的行为线索在工件间传递的程度缺乏量化，亟需一种可测量的语义对齐评估方法。

Method: 提出Desc2Fix框架，采用结构化行为锚点（如复现步骤、API/异常线索、预期vs实际行为）、确定性相似度指标（ROUGE、SBERT、CodeBERT、OpenAI嵌入）以及基于LLM的覆盖度、正确性和特异性判断，在2857个报告-测试-补丁三元组上使用GPT-4o和DeepSeek-Chat进行分析。

Result: LLM能可靠提取结构化信号（完整度达90%），跨模型一致性良好；但对齐高度依赖表示方式，词汇相似度不充分；全diff提供最稳定的报告-补丁对应判断；LLM相对于人类存在系统性乐观偏差（1-2分/5分量表），秩相关性仅中等。

Conclusion: 行为对齐是可测量的但不能简化为相似度，结构化锚点结合嵌入代理可提供可复现的排序和筛选信号，支持更可靠的测试生成、语义感知的故障定位、原则性补丁排序和改进的缺陷报告撰写。

Abstract: Bug resolution is a cross-artifact process: natural-language reports must expose actionable behavioral cues that can be reproduced by tests and corrected by patches. Yet the extent to which these signals are preserved across artifacts remains largely unquantified. We introduce Desc2Fix, a framework for measuring semantic alignment between bug reports, triggering tests, and developer-written fixes. Alignment is operationalized through structured behavioral anchors (e.g., reproduction steps, API/exception cues, expected vs. actual behavior), deterministic similarity metrics (ROUGE, SBERT, CodeBERT, OpenAI embeddings), and LLM-based judgments grounded in coverage, correctness, and specificity. We analyze 2,857 report-test-patch triplets from Defects4J and SWT-Bench using GPT-4o and DeepSeek-Chat. LLMs reliably extract structured signals (up to 90% completeness) and exhibit strong cross-model consistency, yielding a stable semantic input contract for downstream reasoning. However, alignment is highly representation-sensitive: lexical similarity alone is insufficient; full diffs provide the most stable basis for judging report-patch correspondence; and structured summaries trade surface similarity for predicate-level salience. Across more than 182,000 LLM alignment ratings, both models show systematic optimism relative to humans (1-2 points on 5-point scales) and only modest rank agreement, motivating bias-aware evaluation. Our results demonstrate that behavioral alignment is measurable but not reducible to similarity, and that structured anchors combined with embedding-based proxies provide reproducible signals for ranking and filtering tests and candidate patches. By transforming alignment into a controllable engineering signal, Desc2Fix enables more reliable test generation, semantics-aware fault localization, principled patch ranking, and improved bug report authoring.

</details>


### [218] [LM2Alloy: Investigating LLM-Generated Formal Specifications for Automated Test Derivation in Production Software](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18555)
*Tasmim Rashid,Muhammad Zubair Malik*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文探索利用大语言模型（LLM）从需求文档和源代码生成Alloy形式化规约，并从中导出可执行测试用例。在Flipper和Cerberus两个开源Python库上实验，LLM无需人工修正即生成可工作的规约和测试。在Flipper中，该流程发现了一个被现有测试遗漏的真实缺陷（重复flag名），而直接基于文档生成测试（跳过Alloy）虽达68%分支覆盖率却未能发现该bug。Cerberus中，代码推导的规约捕捉到了文档规约遗漏的隐式抽象，生成了额外测试。代码基规约的测试生成方差低于文档基规约。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM能否从需求文档和源代码自动生成形式化规约（Alloy），并利用这些规约生成测试用例，以验证形式化中间表示是否能发现传统测试方法遗漏的约束级缺陷。

Method: 使用LLM从README文档和源代码分别生成Alloy形式化规约，再基于这些规约生成可执行的测试用例；与直接跳过Alloy步骤的基线方法（LLM直接从README生成测试）进行对比。

Result: 1) LLM无需人工修正即可生成可工作的Alloy规约和测试；2) 在Flipper中发现重复flag名bug（现有测试遗漏），而跳过Alloy的基线虽达68%分支覆盖率却未能发现；3) Cerberus中代码基规约捕获了文档遗漏的隐式抽象；4) 代码基规约测试生成方差（SD=2.15）低于文档基（SD=5.0）。

Conclusion: 引入形式化中间表示（Alloy）有助于发现面向覆盖率测试可能遗漏的约束级缺陷；代码基规约能捕捉文档中缺失的隐式语义，且测试生成更稳定。但结论的普适性仍需进一步验证。

Abstract: We present an exploratory study on using Large Language Models (LLMs) to generate Alloy formal specifications from both requirements documentation and production source code, and to derive executable test cases from those specifications. We evaluate on two real open-source Python libraries: Flipper, a feature flag management system, and Cerberus, a data validation library.
  In both cases, the LLM produced workable Alloy specifications and executable tests without any manual correction. For Flipper, our pipeline uncovered a genuine bug that the existing test suite had missed: the library silently accepts duplicate flag names, directly contradicting its documented uniqueness requirement. A direct LLM baseline--generating tests from the same README but skipping the Alloy step--achieved 68% branch coverage yet failed to catch this bug across all three independent runs. This suggests that introducing a formal intermediate representation can surface constraint-level defects that coverage-oriented generation may miss.
  For Cerberus, the code-derived specification captured an implicit abstraction over sized types that the documentation-derived spec omitted, producing two additional tests. Across both libraries, code-based specifications showed lower variance in test generation (mean SD = 2.15) than documentation-based ones (mean SD = 5.0), though whether this generalises remains an open question.
  Index Terms--formal specifications, Alloy, large language models, automated testing, specification drift, software validation.

### [219] [Provably Lossless Acceleration of DNN Mutation Testing via Memoization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18582)
*Ali Ghanbari,Ben Greenman,Sasan Tavakkol,Shibbir Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Mure框架，通过记忆化技术实现无损加速深度神经网络突变测试，平均降低44.54%的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DNN突变测试方法虽然有效但计算成本高昂，已有的加速技术通过有损近似牺牲了突变分数精度，亟需一种无损且高效的加速方法。

Method: Mure基于记忆化思想，识别突变体与原始模型间的共享冗余计算，仅执行每个突变体的突变后缀部分，而复用原始模型中已计算一次的公共前缀部分，并形式化证明了其正确性与加速条件。

Result: 在15个不同架构、复杂度、参数规模从数千到数百万的DNN模型上实验，Mure平均降低44.54%的计算成本；当突变神经元比例高达5%时仍能提供超过20%的加速。

Conclusion: Mure是首个可证明无损的DNN突变测试加速框架，在保证结果等价的同时显著降低计算开销，为大规模DNN测试提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Mutation analysis has recently reemerged in the context of deep neural networks (DNNs) as a promising, but notoriously costly, approach for assessing test dataset adequacy. Existing techniques speed up DNN mutation testing through lossy approximations that trade efficiency for mutation score accuracy. This paper introduces Mure, the first provably lossless framework for accelerating DNN mutation testing via memoization. Mure is based on the idea that DNN mutants and the original model share substantial redundant computation, so during mutation testing, it executes only the mutated suffixes of each mutant and reuses the common prefix from the original model, which is computed only once. We give a formal account of memoized mutation testing, and prove that Mure is sound, i.e., it produces results equivalent to exhaustive vanilla mutation testing, and identify basic conditions under which speed-up is guaranteed. We have implemented Mure and evaluated it on 15 DNN models of various architectures, complexities, and sizes ranging from a few thousands to millions of parameters. This provides empirical evidence that Mure reduces the computational cost of mutation testing by 44.54%, on average. We also observed that while state-of-the-art techniques tend to yield higher acceleration (up to 88.97%, on average), they come at the cost of some error in mutation score. We further analyze the effect of mutation generation selection ratio on the effectiveness of Mure and observed predictable reductions in memoization opportunities with increasing the percentage of mutated neurons. We observed that Mure offers more than 20% speed-up even when as high as 5% of the neurons are mutated.

</details>


### [220] [LLM-Based Invariant Testing for Software Functional Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18711)
*Ruogu Yang,Yifeng He,Yundi Xu,Yuqing Wei,Hao Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LISA，一个基于大语言模型的不变量测试框架，通过迭代生成API序列和程序不变量，结合API n-gram反馈，有效检测软件库中的功能性缺陷，相比传统模糊测试和基于LLM的测试生成方法，具有更高的缺陷检测率和代码覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动编写单元测试耗时且需要深入理解API语义；启发式测试生成方法无法像人类一样推理程序语义或解释源代码和文档；传统模糊测试依赖崩溃检测缺陷，而功能性缺陷不一定会导致崩溃。

Method: LISA框架基于大语言模型，迭代生成API序列和程序不变量，并利用API n-gram反馈来引导测试生成过程。

Result: 相比模糊测试和已有的基于LLM的测试生成方法，LISA实现了更高的缺陷检测率和有竞争力的代码覆盖率，并将每个发现作为高置信度的候选缺陷报告给开发者确认。

Conclusion: LISA有效克服了现有测试生成方法的局限性，为软件库功能性缺陷检测提供了一种高效、高可信度的自动化测试框架。

Abstract: Manually writing unit tests to uncover functional bugs in software libraries is not only time-consuming but also requires a deep understanding of the intended semantics of the APIs. Heuristic-based test generation methods suffer from low usability because they cannot reason about program semantics or interpret source code and documentation as humans do. Traditional fuzzing techniques like OSS-Fuzz often rely on crashes to detect bugs, but functional bugs do not always cause crashes. To overcome these limitations, we present LISA, a novel LLM-based invariant testing framework for software functional bugs. LISA iteratively generates API sequences and program invariants guided by API n-gram feedback, achieving higher bug-detection rates and competitive code coverage compared with both fuzzing and prior LLM-based test generation approaches, and reporting each finding as a high-confidence bug candidate for developer confirmation.

</details>


### [221] [Beyond Text Editing: Algebraic Manipulation of Source Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18742)
*Kevin Pulo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出“源代码代数”这一新型代码编辑范式，通过逻辑代数操作而非纯文本编辑来修改代码，实验表明LLM智能体使用该方法可更高效、更准确地完成跨文件代码变更。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统纯文本编辑方式与代码的语法语义需求之间存在不匹配，尤其在LLM编程智能体时代，将高层计划转化为低层文本编辑代价高昂，需要频繁重新读取大量代码。

Method: 提出源代码代数方法，将代码库修改视为一系列逻辑代数操作序列，每个操作对应一次完整的语义变更（类似于数学方程重写）；定义了组合性、零幂性、交换性等基本性质；开发了概念验证系统SCAS。

Result: 初步可行性实验表明，LLM智能体使用源代码代数完成非局部跨文件代码变更时，成功率更高，且token消耗比基于文本的基线方法少一至两个数量级。

Conclusion: 让LLM输出代数操作而非重写代码是一个有前景的方向，为未来的综合算子库、形式化属性研究和面向人类的工具开发奠定了基础。

Abstract: Source code is almost universally edited as plain text. However, the mismatch between the syntactic and semantic requirements of valid and correct code, and the unconstrained text editing process trying to produce it, introduces friction that degrades the programming task. It is also increasingly costly in the era of LLM-based coding agents, which must materialize their high-level plan of intended changes as low-level text edits dispersed throughout the codebase, often requiring them to re-read large portions of code.
  We propose the novel alternative approach of source code algebra, where the codebase is modified by applying to it a sequence of logical algebraic operations. Each operation makes the full set of changes necessary for a single semantic change, analogous to mathematical equation rewriting. We sketch initial properties of such operations - including composition, nullipotency, and commutativity - that distinguish this approach from text editing, and make it well-suited as a substrate for agentic code editing.
  A feasibility probe with our proof-of-concept implementation (SCAS) suggests that LLM agents can use source code algebra to complete a non-local, cross-file code change with both higher success rates and one to two orders of magnitude fewer tokens, relative to text-based baselines. While preliminary, this is consistent with the hypothesis that having LLMs emit algebraic operations, rather than rewritten code, is a promising direction for code editing - and motivates broader future research into source code algebra, such as comprehensive operator libraries, formal properties, and human-facing tooling.

</details>


### [222] [TrapHunter: Exposing Covert Pathways in Trap Token Contracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18753)
*Yin Wu,Yixuan Liu,Yi Li,Chenyang Peng,Hao Wu,Ming Fan,Ting Liu,Haijun Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出TrapHunter框架，通过意图偏差分析检测伪装成标准代币合约的陷阱合约，在269个真实合约上达到81.8%精度和85.4%召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 攻击者利用标准代币合约（如ERC-20）的标准化特性，通过"欺骗性合规"策略嵌入隐蔽逻辑来欺诈用户，现有检测工具难以发现这类伪装合约。

Method: 首先提出基于代币功能生命周期（生成、流通、持久化、观察）的陷阱分类法；然后构建TrapHunter框架，结合抽象行为树（ABTs）和增强路径图（APGs）进行统一语义表示，利用LLM推理行为意图偏差，并通过分叉动态验证确认可利用性。

Result: 在269个真实合约上使用三种LLM（DeepSeek、GPT、Gemini）进行评估，TrapHunter能有效检测全部六类陷阱，平均精确率81.8%，召回率85.4%，显著优于现有工具。

Conclusion: TrapHunter通过意图偏差分析有效识别标准代币合约中的隐蔽陷阱，为提升数字资产安全性提供了新方法。

Abstract: Standardized token contracts (e.g., ERC-20) form the foundation of digital assets. However, attackers increasingly abuse this standardization to disguise malicious trap tokens. Unlike obvious violations, these contracts employ a strategy of "deceptive adherence": they strictly adhere to standard protocols to evade detection while embedding covert logic to defraud users. To address this, we first systematize the trap landscape by proposing a novel taxonomy derived from the intrinsic functional lifecycle of tokens (Generation, Circulation, Persistence, and Observation). We then propose TrapHunter, a framework designed to identify these traps and expose covert pathways within these deceptive contracts via intent deviation analysis. Specifically, TrapHunter introduces a unified semantic representation combining Abstract Behavior Trees (ABTs) and Augmented Path Graphs (APGs) to normalize intra-procedural syntax and reveal hidden execution paths driven by inter-procedural state dependencies. Crucially, it bridges the semantic gap by leveraging LLMs to reason about the behavioral intent of deviations from reference implementations, followed by fork-based dynamic validation to confirm exploitability. Experimental evaluation on 269 real-world contracts with three LLMs (DeepSeek, GPT, and Gemini) demonstrates that TrapHunter effectively detects all six categories of traps, achieving an average precision of 81.8% and recall of 85.4%, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art tools.

### [223] [TraceDev: A Traceability-Driven Multi-agent Framework for Requirement-to-Code Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18886)
*Mingyu Chen,Yakun Zhang,Zihao Xie,Yixing Luo,Jinrui Xu,Cuiyun Gao,Kaiqi Zhao,Yunming Ye*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖简化指令（如单句描述），无法反映复杂软件开发场景，且缺乏明确的需求可追溯机制，难以精确对齐和验证生成代码与原始需求。

Method: 提出TraceDev多智能体框架，包含五个角色智能体（需求细化者、设计者、开发者、测试者、验证者）。验证者智能体构建并维护异构可追踪图，链接需求、设计模型和代码工件，与其它四个智能体交互，保持各工件间一致性并作为结构化上下文支持高效内存管理。

Result: 在ETOUR数据集上成功率达53.63%，优于基线方法最高186.63%；在SMOS数据集上成功率达56.82%，优于基线方法最高340.80%。

Conclusion: TraceDev在从需求进行仓库级代码生成方面是有效的。

Abstract: In modern software development, the rapid advancement of Large Language Models (LLMs) has made the end-to-end transformation of Natural Language Requirements (NLRs) into executable repository-level code increasingly feasible. However, existing approaches typically rely on simplified instructions (e.g., single-sentence descriptions), failing to reflect complex software development scenarios. Moreover, they lack explicit requirement traceability mechanisms, making it difficult to precisely align and validate generated code against original requirements. To address these limitations, we propose TraceDev, a multi-agent framework for automated software development grounded in use cases that contain multiple functional points and complex semantics. TraceDev employs five role-specific agents, including a Requirement Refiner, Designer, Developer, Tester, and Validator. Notably, the Validator Agent constructs and maintains a heterogeneous traceability graph that links requirements, design models, and code artifacts for interacting with the preceding four agents. The traceability graph maintains consistency across various artifacts and serves as a structured context for efficient memory management, supporting reliable repository-level code generation. We evaluate TraceDev on two widely used datasets (including 125 use cases) compared with two state-of-the-art approaches. On the ETOUR dataset, TraceDev achieves a success rate of 53.63\%, outperforming baseline approaches by up to 186.63\%. A similar trend is observed on the SMOS dataset, where TraceDev attains a success rate of 56.82\%, exceeding baseline approaches by up to 340.80\%. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of TraceDev in repository-level code generation from requirements.

### [224] [Skillware: A Software Ontology and Engineering Lifecycle for Persistent Behavioral Artifacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18970)
*Haodi Fan,Zucong Lan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Skillware概念，将AI代理系统中的技能行为定义为独立软件工件，包含行为优先性、独立软件身份和代理主机执行关系三个必要条件，并通过生命周期连续性管理其演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究解释了Agent Skills的规范、执行、维护和演化，但缺乏将这些行为工件定义为独立软件对象的本体论，导致技能无法作为可识别、可组合、可维护和可演化的软件工件进行管理。

Method: 定义Skillware软件抽象，包含Skill Artifact（可复用任务行为规范）和Skillware Unit（管理工件的独立身份与生命周期），提出三个必要条件（行为优先性、独立软件身份、Agent Host执行关系）和生命周期连续性属性，并结合Agent Skills规范、138,133条SKILL.md记录、15个边界案例和13个工程实现进行验证。

Result: 证据表明存在重复出现的工件包络、可分离的软件身份、兼容的执行路径以及生命周期工程压力，验证了Skillware作为软件本体和工程框架的有效性。

Conclusion: Skillware提供了软件本体论和工程生命周期，使AI代理能力能够成为可识别、可组合、可维护和可演化的软件工件，填补了Agent Skills缺乏独立软件对象定义的空白。

Abstract: Agent Skills have become persistent behavioral artifacts across independent AI agent systems. They combine natural-language task specifications with metadata and optional references, scripts, assets, hooks, package manifests, tests, and companion interfaces. Existing studies explain how Skills are specified, executed, maintained, and evolved, but lack an ontology that defines these artifacts as independent software objects. This paper introduces Skillware as the software abstraction that extends software engineering to persistent Behavioral Artifacts in agent systems. A Skill Artifact specifies reusable task behavior; a Skillware Unit manages that artifact as software through an independent identity and lifecycle. A compatible Agent Host activates the unit for runtime interpretation. Three necessary conditions operationalize category membership: behavioral primacy, independent software identity, and an Agent Host execution relationship. Lifecycle Continuity records whether the same unit identity persists through update, maintenance, rollback, and removal as a separate software-grade property. Evidence combines the Agent Skills specification, a frozen corpus of 138,133 content-deduplicated SKILL.md records associated with 20,556 repository identifiers, independent empirical studies, 15 category-boundary cases, and 13 fixed-revision engineering implementations. The evidence establishes a recurring artifact envelope, separable software identities, compatible execution paths, and lifecycle engineering pressure. Skillware provides the software ontology and engineering lifecycle through which agent capabilities can become identifiable, composable, maintainable, and evolvable software artifacts.

### [225] [From Collaboration to Regulation: Characterizing Governance Practice in Three Deep Learning Open Source Communities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19022)
*Ruiqiao Qiu,Wenhao Yang,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对PyTorch、TensorFlow和Paddle三个成熟深度学习框架的混合方法实证研究，分析了109份治理文档和1700多次提交，识别出17个规则主题和33项可操作的治理实践，揭示了开源软件项目中治理规则的演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源软件项目面临协调和质量控制挑战，维护者缺乏关于何时制定、修订规则以及如何组织治理文档的系统性指导。

Method: 采用混合方法实证研究，基于制度分析与发展(IAD)框架，分析109份治理文档和1700多次代码提交，识别规则主题和治理功能。

Result: 识别出17个规则主题（7种类型），发现操作性规则（如工作流）出现更早、修订更频繁，结构性规则（如角色层级）出现较晚、变化较少；规则内容逐渐向任务和角色特定文件专业化。

Conclusion: 总结出33项针对成熟大型开源软件项目的可操作治理实践，涵盖规则类型、时间安排和组织方式。

Abstract: Collaboration in Open Source Software (OSS) projects creates substantial coordination and quality-control challenges across diverse contributor bases. Projects address these challenges through documented governance rules, yet maintainers have limited systematic guidance on what rules to codify, when to introduce or revise them, and how to organize them across documents. We conducted a mixed-methods empirical study of three mature deep learning frameworks: PyTorch, TensorFlow, and Paddle. Using the Institutional Analysis and Development framework, we analyzed 109 documents and identified 17 rule themes across seven rule types. Operational rules, such as workflows, appeared across all three projects, whereas structural rules, such as role hierarchies, varied more substantially. Tracing more than 1,700 commits, we found that operational rule themes generally appeared earlier and were revised more frequently, while many structural rule themes emerged later and changed less often. Rule-bearing content also became increasingly specialized across task- and role-specific files. We further identified four governance functions reflected in substantive rule changes: Norm Alignment, Workflow Refinement, Coordination Structuring, and Community and Governance Development. Synthesizing these findings, we derive 33 actionable governance practices for mature, large-scale OSS projects with substantial coordination demands and organizational involvement.

### [226] [SciCodePile: A 128GB Corpus and Executable Benchmark for Challenging Scientific Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19104)
*Weifeng Sun,Ye Fan,Yuchen Chen,Gou Tan,Jieke Shi,Yuan Yidi,Swee Liang Wong,Jonathan Pan,David Lo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文构建了迄今为止最大的科学代码语料库SciCodePile（128GB/3.7万仓库），并从中筛选出200个可执行评测任务。评估15个LLM发现科学代码生成极具挑战性（最佳CodeBLEU仅38.13，Pass@1仅12.30%），而基于该语料库的继续预训练和指令微调能显著提升性能（CodeBLEU提升2.84倍，Pass@1提升4.79倍）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学代码数据集规模小、领域覆盖有限、缺乏可执行验证，无法准确评估LLM在科学代码生成上的真实能力缺口。

Method: 从3.7万个公开仓库构建128GB科学代码语料库，筛选200个可执行任务（配备沙箱执行环境和自动化测试），在15个LLM上评估前缀补全、中间填充和可执行代码生成三项任务。

Result: 最佳模型在两项补全任务上CodeBLEU仅38.13和38.37，可执行基准Pass@1仅12.30%；但继续预训练提升CodeBLEU 2.84倍，指令微调提升Pass@1 4.79倍。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在科学代码生成上远未达到可靠水平，而SciCodePile语料库作为资源和训练数据能有效提升模型性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at general-purpose code generation, yet how well they handle scientific code remains an open question. Existing datasets and benchmarks are limited in scale, domain coverage, or executable verification, leaving the true gap between current LLMs and reliable scientific code generators inadequately assessed. To address these limitations, we present SciCodePile, the largest scientific code corpus to date, constructed from 37,737 public repositories and collectively comprising 128GB of code that spans multiple computational science disciplines. From this corpus, we further curate an executable benchmark of 200 tasks, each equipped with a sandboxed execution environment and an automated test harness for functional verification. We evaluate 15 LLMs from both open-source and closed-source families on three tasks: prefix-to-suffix completion, fill-in-the-middle infilling, and executable code generation. Results show that scientific code generation remains highly challenging: The best CodeBLEU reaches only 38.13 and 38.37 on the two completion tasks, while the strongest model achieves just 12.30\% Pass@1 on the executable benchmark, underscoring how far current models remain from reliable scientific code generation. To demonstrate the training utility of SciCodePile, we further show that continued pretraining on our corpus improves CodeBLEU by $\times$2.84 on scientific code completion, and instruction tuning on our data improves Pass@1 by $\times$4.79 on the executable benchmark. All code and data are available at https://huggingface.co/SciCodePile.

### [227] [EmbeddedKittens: An Evaluation of Code Embeddings for Scratch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19291)
*Benedikt Fein,Gordon Fraser*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管代码嵌入在机器学习中广泛应用，但哪种嵌入方法最适合编程教育中的学习分析仍是开放问题。特别是针对Scratch这类可视化积木式编程语言，现有的自然语言处理方法无法直接应用。

Method: 作者实例化了四种大语言模型和五种不同的Scratch程序嵌入方法，构建了标记预测任务和两种不同的分类任务及对应数据集，并进行了实证评估。

Result: 代码嵌入可以成功迁移到Scratch教育环境中。基于大规模开源Scratch数据集训练的嵌入模型能够捕获相关的结构和语义信息，在典型的小规模课堂场景中无需任务特定的模型微调即可实现学习分析（如预测学生程序的功能正确性）。

Conclusion: 代码嵌入方法在编程教育领域具有可行性和有效性，为基于积木式编程语言的学习分析提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: The trend of embedding source code for machine learning applications also enables new opportunities in learning analytics in programming education, but which code embedding approach is most suitable for learning analytics remains an open question. A common approach to embedding source code lies in treating the code as a token sequence similar to natural language when training large language models~(LLMs). However, in case of visual block-based programming languages like Scratch, this approach cannot be applied directly. While text-based representations of block-based code can be created to apply LLMs to this problem, other dedicated embedding models could potentially exhibit improved performance by capturing additional structural information. In this paper, we therefore instantiate four LLMs and five different popular embedding approaches for Scratch programs, create a token-prediction and two different classification tasks with corresponding datasets, and empirically evaluate the models on them. Our experiments demonstrate that a transfer of code embeddings to the educational environment of Scratch is feasible. The embedding models trained on large open Scratch datasets capture relevant structural and semantic information about the code to enable learning analytics like predicting functional correctness of student programs, in the typically small classroom setting without requiring further task-specific model fine-tuning.
